<span id="freeTextContainer6683461036667093007"><i> "Everything was going exactly to plan. And that was exactly why she didn't trust it." </i><br/><br/>3.5 ⭐️<br/><br/>I didn't find myself as invested in this book as the first one, it took longer for me to become gripped. I didn't like Kate's character very much in this one, she came across as arrogant and rude and times.<br/><br/>In Our Dark Duet, Kate and August are living entirely different lives. August is living in Verity - building an army in order to fight the monsters who work for Sloan. And the numbers of monsters seem </span>
  <span id="freeText6683461036667093007" style="display:none"><i> "Everything was going exactly to plan. And that was exactly why she didn't trust it." </i><br /><br />3.5 ⭐️<br /><br />I didn't find myself as invested in this book as the first one, it took longer for me to become gripped. I didn't like Kate's character very much in this one, she came across as arrogant and rude and times.<br /><br />In Our Dark Duet, Kate and August are living entirely different lives. August is living in Verity - building an army in order to fight the monsters who work for Sloan. And the numbers of monsters seem to be growing every day. <br />Kate is in Prosperity, trying to forget Verity, forget her past and start again. But it is harder said than done, and eventually Kate realises she must return to Verity. <br /><br />It is pretty action packed, there is plenty going on plot wise. I'm not sure, but the characters just weren't enough for me. I was entertained, but not enthralled.<br /><br /><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ I didn't like that Kate left her friends in Prosperity and then because of her death she will never see them again. In fact they wouldn't even have known she had died - which was a bit shit. Also I didn't like the relationship between her and August but that's no surprise of course.  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br />If you enjoy the supernatural, and an easy fast paced read then I recommend. <br /><br /></span>

<div id="review_1719782239" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1719782239" />
    <a title="Simona B" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5312173-simona-b"><img alt="Simona B" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1408893128p2/5312173.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1719782239?book_show_action=true">Jun 12, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Simona B" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Simona B" href="/user/show/5312173-simona-b">Simona B</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Paperback 9781785652769" href="/book/show/34397653-our-dark-duet">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5312173-simona-b?shelf=2000">2000</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5312173-simona-b?shelf=in-english">in-english</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5312173-simona-b?shelf=fantastic-lit-and-co">fantastic-lit-and-co</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1719782239" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16003963904063341238"><b>“So often, living hurt.”</b><br/><br/><b>3.5</b> maybe? Something between that and <b>4</b> stars, anyway.<br/><br/>•I must admit,<b> I didn't remember much from <i>This Savage Song</i></b>. It was easy to brush everything up once I got started, but the first pages had me a little lost. And then something strange happened: my <b>difficulty to get in sync with the story </b>remained, only<b> its cause </b>shifted from my temporary lack of basic information to something that I'm still not really able to pinpoint with precision, but that is most definitely <b>intern</b></span>
  <span id="freeText16003963904063341238" style="display:none"><b>“So often, living hurt.”</b><br /><br /><b>3.5</b> maybe? Something between that and <b>4</b> stars, anyway.<br /><br />•I must admit,<b> I didn't remember much from <i>This Savage Song</i></b>. It was easy to brush everything up once I got started, but the first pages had me a little lost. And then something strange happened: my <b>difficulty to get in sync with the story </b>remained, only<b> its cause </b>shifted from my temporary lack of basic information to something that I'm still not really able to pinpoint with precision, but that is most definitely <b>internal</b> to the book. <br />I know I'm difficult to follow. That's kind of my thing. Just bear with me. <br /><br />•I think <b>the best stories are the ones where the artifice is least evident</b>. Of course we all know fictional stories always are the children of someone's mind. And of course we accept that without giving it even half a thought: suspension of disbelief, narrative covenant, call it what you will, the core doesn't change: <b>I'll happily believe anything as long as you don't allow me to notice it's all a lie</b>. Now, I think <i>Our Dark Duet</i> misses this fundamental target <b>when it comes to the storyline</b>—but mind you, the storyline and nothing else. The rest is as perfect as we've learned to expect from the one and only Victoria Schwab, and sure enough, unsurprisingly, I enjoyed it. But <b>the plot was somewhat awkward, it couldn't hold my attention, and it even bored me</b>, which is a first for me, with Schwab's name in the equation. <br /><br />•An instance could be towards the end, when Kate <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[leaves the Compound to chase after Alice when she knows it's a trap, the whole crew goes after her, Henry is captured during the action, and three minutes later, they all (minus Henry) are home again <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>. Like<b> I'm not supposed to notice </b>the whole sequence is just an excuse to <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[get Henry into Sloan's hands <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>?<br />This is only the clearest example I can think of, but I perceived this effect more or less throughout the whole book. It was as if <b>the frame of the plot</b>, which should be invisible, <b>showed through </b>all the time. It sounds so futile a thing, but if you think about it, those are always the ones that really ruin it. And probably, had the author been anyone else, I wouldn't have even noticed it.<br /><br />•<b>The ending</b> is a big yes for me. <b>Poignant, beautiful, absolutely heart-rending</b>, and <b>sadly necessary</b>. (Leigh, Bardugo, just so you know, this is how you <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[kill a main character in the last pages <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>. I love your books but on this you should take some notes.)<br /><br />➽ <b><i>Our Dark Duet</i> surely is a worthy conclusion</b> to one of the best YA series out there, and I can only recommend it wholeheartedly. But Schwab's name on the cover alone should be enough to melt your doubts like snow in the sun-</span>
  <a data-text-id="16003963904063341238" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<span id="freeTextContainer6828499517708352360">I won't be reviewing this but I did want to leave a small thought or two. <br/>The book wasn't bad--it was a grey finale and I think if you liked <i>This Savage Song</i>, you'll like this one too.   <span id="freeText6828499517708352360" style="display:none">I won't be reviewing this but I did want to leave a small thought or two. <br />The book wasn't bad--it was a grey finale and I think if you liked <i>This Savage Song</i>, you'll like this one too. <div id="review_2049662921" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2049662921" />
    <a title="Misstdennis" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/41744660-misstdennis"><img alt="Misstdennis" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1570069040p2/41744660.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2049662921?book_show_action=true">Jul 04, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Misstdennis" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Misstdennis" href="/user/show/41744660-misstdennis">Misstdennis</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Paperback 9781785652769" href="/book/show/34397653-our-dark-duet">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/41744660-misstdennis?shelf=owned-books">owned-books</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2049662921" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16888836703419808856"><b>5000/5 stars</b><br/>Obviously...<br/><br/><i>“Mourning was its own kind of music—the sound of so many hearts, of so many breaths, of so many standing together.”</i><br/><br/>Hey <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/3099544.Victoria_Schwab' title='Victoria Schwab' rel='nofollow noopener'>Victoria Schwab</a>, is it okay if I refer you as <b>Sloan</b> for now on? That's okay? Cool.<br/>You sadistic human being...<br/><br/>9 hours it took me to read this book. And in 9 hours, I didn't breath, eat, drink or feel my heart beating.<br/><b>Not once.</b><br/><br/>That book was just something else. I'm legitimately struggling for words because I'm trying to hold myself together, <i>but I'm failing</i></span>
  <span id="freeText16888836703419808856" style="display:none"><b>5000/5 stars</b><br />Obviously...<br /><br /><i>“Mourning was its own kind of music—the sound of so many hearts, of so many breaths, of so many standing together.”</i><br /><br />Hey <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/3099544.Victoria_Schwab" title="Victoria Schwab" rel="nofollow noopener">Victoria Schwab</a>, is it okay if I refer you as <b>Sloan</b> for now on? That's okay? Cool.<br />You sadistic human being...<br /><br />9 hours it took me to read this book. And in 9 hours, I didn't breath, eat, drink or feel my heart beating.<br /><b>Not once.</b><br /><br />That book was just something else. I'm legitimately struggling for words because I'm trying to hold myself together, <i>but I'm failing miserably</i>.<br />My hands are shaking, I'm having heart palpitations and I just cannot for the life of me think of anything over the sound of heartache.<br /><b>Someone call emergency!</b><br />Because of all this, I apologise to you in advance for this review as I cannot guarantee that this will be in any way, decent. <br /><br />I said this in my review for <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/23299512.This_Savage_Song__Monsters_of_Verity___1_" title="This Savage Song (Monsters of Verity, #1) by Victoria Schwab" rel="nofollow noopener">This Savage Song</a>, where I mentioned that I always find it hard to not compare <b>A Darker Shade of Magic</b> to her other books, but to be honest, this one might come close, <i>so very close</i> to topping that trilogy.<br />I mean, an urban dystopian and maybe a bit of fantasy setting, music, monsters<i>(who are <b>ugly AF</b>)</i> completely and utterly perfect characters. <br />What more could you need?<br /><br />The way Victoria Schwab <i>AKA Sloan,</i> constructs her stories is just so beautiful. It's also beautiful when she throws you head first into a raging pit of fire that leaves you feeling so numb afterwards. So please, to anyone who still hasn't picked up this duology, just stop what you're doing, put your life on hold and as Shia Labeouf would say, <b>JUST DO IT!</b> and allow her to throw you into that raging pit of fire.<br /><br />I'm so sad this we have seen the end of this series and that I'll won't see more of these beautiful, beautiful characters, but honestly, I'm pretty glad. I don't know if I'd come out alive after reading more. I barely made it out alive today...<br /><br /><i>“I know it hurts," she said. "So make it worth the pain.”</i><br /><br />I just want to sit and use this moment to pay my respects and appreciation for the characters for a brief moment.<br />Brief, because I don't have it in my to dive into too much rambling after that <b>fucking ending.</b><br />fuck.<br /><br /><b>Kate</b> and <b>August</b> both had such a huge character development in this book and I feel like it needs to be at least acknowledged. <br /><i>Don't worry, this is a spoiler free review.</i><br />I absolutely <b>adored</b> Kate and August, I really love them in this book, maybe even more so this time around, and their development in this was so great to see, but my one true love and trophy winning for this book is <b>Ilsa.</b> <i>My baby, I love you, you sweet red-head girl</i>. Out of everyone, I feel like she takes the cake in character development.<br />If I wasn't convinced throughout the book, that ending alone as made it so clear.<br /><br />I'm not going to delve into the plot of the book, because honestly, you should just read it for yourself and find out.<br /><i>hahahahaha good luck</i><br /><br />Never reading a Victoria Shwab book again.<br /><b>Ever.</b><br /><br />Jokes baby, I love you.</span>
  <a data-text-id="16888836703419808856" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('PEWuRHkFfrPHa/BQ8iKzk2G8z88NApTwbS3aN1yPriU/Tn1ORxEuGEf0HOIApIAYa+KM3ihBYqqlbUQ26L9GlQ==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('9pZCjPwLvzUS4mFmH8Xqo32ERiIB0t52jGLs4cmKkQ/1nZGGwh/vnpJ9jdTtQ9kod9oFMySRKCxEInLgfbp5vw==')})
  }

          $$('div.prototip').each(function(i){i.setStyle({zIndex: 6000})});
        }
      });

      newTip['wrapper'].addClassName('prototipAllowOverflow');

        $('bookCover_40642172').observe('prototip:shown', function () {
          $$('div.prototip').each(function (e) {
            if ($('bookCover_40642172').hasClassName('ignored')) {
              e.setStyle({'display': 'none'});
              return;
            }
            e.setStyle({'overflow': 'visible'});
          });
        });
      $('bookCover_40642172').observe('prototip:hidden', function () {
        $$('span.elementTwo').each(function (e) {
          if (e.getStyle('display') !== 'none') {
            var lessLink = e.next();
            swapContent(lessLink);
          }
        });
      });

//]]>
</script>

</li>
</ul>
